function loadCarouselProducts(tabName, currentTab) {
	var screenWidth = screen.width;
	 if('search' =='homepage') {

		 $.ajax({
		 	  url: "/home/getCarouselProducts?activeTab="+tabName,
		 	  success: function(data) {
		 		  var currentHtml;
		 		  if(screenWidth < 960) {
			 			if(currentTab === undefined){
			 				currentTab = "accessibletabscontent0-0";
			 			}
			 			$("#"+currentTab).addClass('active');
			 			$("#"+currentTab).next().find('.carousel__component').html(data);
			 	   		$("#"+currentTab).next().find('.js-owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
			  				afterInit : showProductCarouselNow,
			  				navigation:true,
			  				navigationText : ["<span class='icon-arrow-left'></span>", "<span class='icon-arrow-right'></span>"],
			  				pagination:false,
			  				itemsCustom : [[0, 1], [640, 3], [1024, 4], [1400, 5]],
			  				mouseDrag : false,
			  			});
						currentHtml=currentTab;
			 		  }

		 		 if(screenWidth >= 960) {
		 			 $("#landingCarouselDiv .carousel__component").html(data);
			 		 $('#landingCarouselDiv .js-owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
			 				afterInit : showProductCarouselNow,
			 				navigation:true,
			 				navigationText : ["<span class='icon-arrow-left'></span>", "<span class='icon-arrow-right'></span>"],
			 				pagination:false,
			 				itemsCustom : [[0, 1], [640, 3], [1024, 4], [1400, 5]],
			 				mouseDrag : false,
			 		});
					 currentHtml="#landingCarouselDiv .carousel__component";
		 		  }

		 		  $(".initspindisplay").css("display","block");

		 	  ACC.product.enableAddToCartAmountComponent();
		 	  ACC.product.addtoMyList();

		               var f = e.toString().replace(",", ".");
		               return $.isNumeric(f) ? ($(this).val(f), ACC.product.changeProductAmountInCard(c, "validateuserinput", ACC.product.getUnitIndex(b), d), a.preventDefault(), !1) : (a.preventDefault(), !1)
		           }), $(".tabs-responsive .amountinput").on("change", function(a) {

ACC.product.changeProductAmountInCard(f, "validateuserinputgram", ACC.product.getUnitIndex(c), e) : ACC.product.changeProductAmountInCard(f, "validateuserinput", ACC.product.getUnitIndex(c), e))
		               }, 100)

		           }), $(".tabs-responsive .poids").on("click", function(a) {

		               $(this).parent("div").find(".pieces").removeAttr("disabled");
		               $(this).parent("div").find(".pieces").removeClass("active");
		               $(this).hasClass("active") || ($(this).addClass("active"), $("#productid-" + b).find(".spinner .poids").addClass("active"), $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled"), d.attr("disabled", "disabled"), d.removeClass("active"), $("#productid-" + b).find(".spinner .pieces").removeClass("active"), a.detail && 1 != a.detail || (unitindex = parseInt($(this).data("index")), ACC.product.changeProductAmountInCard(c, "changegram", unitindex, b)))
		           })
		 	  } ,
		 	  error: function(xhr) {
		 	  }
		 	});
	 }
}
</script>

<script>

if(screen.width < 960) {
	$(document).delegate("#landingCarouselDiv .tabhead","click",function(event){
		 var tabID = $(this).attr('id');
		 var dataActiveVal = $(this).attr('data-active-value');
		 if($(this).hasClass('active')) {
			 $("#landingCarouselDiv .tabhead").removeClass('active');
			 $("#landingCarouselDiv .tabhead").parent().find('.tabbody').hide();
			 $(this).removeClass('active');
			 $(this).parent().find('.tabbody').hide();
		 } else {
			 $("#landingCarouselDiv .tabhead").removeClass('active');
			 $("#landingCarouselDiv .tabhead").parent().find('.tabbody').hide();
			 $(this).addClass('active');
			 $(this).parent().find('.tabbody').show();
			 loadCarouselProducts(dataActiveVal, tabID);
		 }


	});
}

</script>

    (function () {
        window.__gigyaConf = JSON.parse('{"enabledProviders":"*","sessionExpiration":604800}');
        var gig = document.createElement('script');
        gig.type = 'text/javascript';
        gig.async = true;
        gig.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://cdns' : 'http://cdn') + '.gigya.com/js/gigya.js?apiKey=3_PkRDAT7GxAxa1vjGHqtidhtBzz27gVdjsdlB5X0utnCqzMTQ_mfklMEx-hnqg2b3&lang=nl';
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(gig);
        window.__gigyaApiKey = '3_PkRDAT7GxAxa1vjGHqtidhtBzz27gVdjsdlB5X0utnCqzMTQ_mfklMEx-hnqg2b3';
        window.__gigyaConfName = 'gigyacloudserviceconfigPROD';

    function gigyaChecklogout() {
		var createCookie = function(name, value, days) {
            if (days) {
                var date = new Date();
                date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
            }
            else var expires = "";

            document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
        };
        var readCookie = function(name) {
            var nameEQ = name + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
            }
            return null;
        };
        var eraseCookie = function(name) {
            createCookie(name, "", -1);
        }
		if (readCookie("gigyaLogout") === "true") {
            gigya.accounts.logout();
			eraseCookie("gigyaLogout");
        }
    }
    function onGigyaServiceReady(serviceName) {
        gigyaChecklogout();
        if (window.gigyaInit) {
            var length = window.gigyaInit.length,
                    element = null;
            if (length > 0) {
                for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                    element = window.gigyaInit[i];
                    func = element.function;
                    var parts = func.split("\.");
                    var f = gigya[parts[0]][parts[1]];
                    if (typeof f === "function") {
                        f(element.parameters);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (window.gigyaAem.functions.raasOnLoginCallback) {
                gigya.accounts.addEventHandlers(
                        {
                            onLogin: window.gigyaAem.functions.raasOnLoginCallback
                        }
                )
            }
        }
    }

</script>

            <script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {

        // gestion du gif de chargement
        var currentNavJSON = "navigation";
        //chargement terminer
        function FinishLoadingDone(){
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event':'async_components_loaded'
            })
        };
        //chargement des donnée JSON
        $.ajax({
          type: "GET",
          dataType: "json",
          url: "https://www.carrefour.be/content/dam/carrefour/freehtml/nav/" +currentNavJSON+ ".json", // Using our resources.json file to serve result
          success: function(site) {
            var encodedStringAtoBNav = 'RGF0ZU9mUHJldmlldw==';
            // Decode the String
            var decodedStringAtoBNav = atob(encodedStringAtoBNav);

            var outputDateOfDayNav = new Date();

            var outputLangueNav = $("html").attr("lang");
            console.log("chargement nav");
            var navItem = "";
            if( outputLangueNav == "fr" ){
                    //Nav Banner generation
                    for (var i in site) {
                        var actualdateinNav = new Date(site[i].datein);
                        var actualdateoutNav = new Date(site[i].dateout);
                        if( site[i].publish == true && actualdateinNav <=  outputDateOfDayNav && actualdateoutNav > outputDateOfDayNav ){
                            //console.log( "titre "+ site[i].brand );
                            var checkTargetUrlNav = site[i].targetblank;
                            var checkNewTargetUrlNav ="";
                            if( checkTargetUrlNav == true ){ checkNewTargetUrlNav = "target='_blank'" }
                            navItem ="<div class='promo-image-container d-flex flex-column justify-content-start align-items-center'>"+
                                        "    <a class='d-flex flex-row justify-content-center align-items-center w-100 pb-0 px-3 pt-3' " +checkNewTargetUrlNav  + " href='" + site[i].urlfr +"'>"+
                                        "        <span class='img-container image_fit_2_1 w-100'>"+
                                        "            <img class='w-100 showCursor' alt='" + site[i].altimgfr +"' src='https://cdn-mkt.be.carrefour.eu/free-html/navigation/" + site[i].imgfr +"'>"+
                                        "        </span>"+
                                        "    </a>"+
                                        "</div>";
                            if( site[i].bioforme == true ){ $("#BioForme-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].produitsfrais == true ){ $("#ProduitsFrais-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].epicerie == true ){ $("#Epicerie-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].boissons == true ){ $("#Boissons-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].surgeles == true ){ $("#Surgeles-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].bebe == true ){ $("#Bebe-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].soinshygiene == true ){ $("#SoinsHygiene-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].entretien == true ){ $("#Entretien-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].nonalimentaire == true ){ $("#NonAlimentaire-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].bedr918000000000000 == true ){ $("#BEDR918000000000000-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                        }
                    }
            }
            if( outputLangueNav == "nl" ){
                    //Nav Banner generation
                    for (var i in site) {
                        var actualdateinNav = new Date(site[i].datein);
                        var actualdateoutNav = new Date(site[i].dateout);
                        if( site[i].publish == true && actualdateinNav <=  outputDateOfDayNav && actualdateoutNav > outputDateOfDayNav ){
                            var checkTargetUrlNav = site[i].targetblank;
                            var checkNewTargetUrlNav ="";
                            if( checkTargetUrlNav == true ){ checkNewTargetUrlNav = "target='_blank'" }
                            navItem ="<div class='promo-image-container d-flex flex-column justify-content-start align-items-center'>"+
                                        "    <a class='d-flex flex-row justify-content-center align-items-center w-100 pb-0 px-3 pt-3' " +checkNewTargetUrlNav  + " href='" + site[i].urlnl +"'>"+
                                        "        <span class='img-container image_fit_2_1 w-100'>"+
                                        "            <img class='w-100 showCursor ' alt='" + site[i].altimgnl +"' src='https://cdn-mkt.be.carrefour.eu/free-html/navigation/" + site[i].imgnl +"'>"+
                                        "        </span>"+
                                        "    </a>"+
                                        "</div>";
                            if( site[i].bioforme == true ){ $("#BioForme-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].produitsfrais == true ){ $("#ProduitsFrais-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].epicerie == true ){ $("#Epicerie-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].boissons == true ){ $("#Boissons-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].surgeles == true ){ $("#Surgeles-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].bebe == true ){ $("#Bebe-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].soinshygiene == true ){ $("#SoinsHygiene-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].entretien == true ){ $("#Entretien-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].nonalimentaire == true ){ $("#NonAlimentaire-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                            if( site[i].bedr918000000000000 == true ){ $("#BEDR918000000000000-content .card-body").append(navItem);}
                        }
                    }
            }
        },
          complete: function() {
            FinishLoadingDone();
          },
          error: function( site ) {
              console.log( "ERROR:  " + site );
          }
        });

});

<script>
    (function() {
        window.isLoggedIn = false;
        window.gig_login_response = "";
        window.onGigyaServiceReady = function() {
            if (!window.gigya || !window.gigya.accounts) {
                return;
            }
            console.log('Gigya Service Ready');
            gigya.hasSession().then(
                function(sessionExists){
                    console.log('Gigya hasSession callback', sessionExists);
                    // OSM-8753/OSC-18682 :: storepicker disappearing issue fix
                    // global opbject had missing isUserLoggedIn function. Added check with interval
                    var functionCheckInterval;
                    functionCheckInterval = setInterval(() => {
                        if(typeof isUserLoggedIn === 'function'){
                            clearInterval(functionCheckInterval);
                            isUserLoggedIn(sessionExists);
                        }
                    }, 200);
                    // isUserLoggedIn(sessionExists);
            });

            var oseGigyaInterval = setInterval(function() {
                if (typeof oseGigyaHybris !== 'undefined') {
                    //OSC-18554 SAP CDC has.Session() integration
                    console.log("OSE function called oseGigyaHybris");
                    oseGigyaHybris.init();
                    clearInterval(oseGigyaInterval);
                }
            }, 500);

            window.gigya.accounts.getJWT({
                fields: 'email,data.carrefour.personuid,data.carrefour.accountuid,data.loyalty.card',
                callback: function callback(response) {
                    if (response.status === 'OK' && response.id_token) {

                        window.isLoggedIn = true;
                        window.gig_login_response = response;

                    } else {
                        window.isLoggedIn = false;
                    }

                }
            });

            //gigyaChecklogout();
            if (window.gigyaInit) {
                var length = window.gigyaInit.length,
                    element = null;
                if (length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                        element = window.gigyaInit[i];
                        func = element.function;
                        var parts = func.split("\.");
                        var f = gigya[parts[0]][parts[1]];
                        if (typeof f === "function") {
                            f(element.parameters);
                        }
                    }
                }
                if(window.gigyaAem != undefined){
                    if (window.gigyaAem.functions.raasOnLoginCallback) {
                        gigya.accounts.addEventHandlers({
                            onLogin: window.gigyaAem.functions.raasOnLoginCallback
                        })
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

	<script>
				$.widget("custom.tooltipX", $.ui.tooltip, {
			     options: {
			      autoHide: true
			    },

			    _create: function () {
			      this._super();
			      if (!this.options.autoHide) {
			        this._off(this.element, "mouseover focusin");
			      }
			    },

			    _open: function (event, target, content) {
			      this._superApply(arguments);

			      if (!this.options.autoHide) {
			        this._off(this.element, "mouseleave focusout");
			      }
			    }
			  });
$( document ).ready(function() {

   if($('body').hasClass('page-homepage') || $('body').hasClass('page-productDetails') || $('body').hasClass('page-productList') || $('body').hasClass('page-search')) {
			var otherPages=$('.owl-carousel__without');
			var isOtherPages=otherPages.length;
			function showHomepageCarousel(elem){
				if(isOtherPages){
					var innerChildElement=otherPages.find('.item');
					if(innerChildElement.length){
						innerChildElement.wrap('<div class="owl-item">');
					}
					var owlItemElement=otherPages.find('.owl-item');
					if(owlItemElement.length){
						owlItemElement.wrap('<div class="owl-wrapper">');
					}
					var owlWrapperElement=otherPages.find('.owl-wrapper');
					if(owlWrapperElement.length){
						owlWrapperElement.wrap('<div class="owl-wrapper-outer">');
					}
				}
				var owlitems = $('.owl-carousel__specific,.owl-carousel__without').find('.owl-item');
				if(owlitems.length == 1){
					//$('.upscontainer').css('margin-top', '58px');
					$('.owl-wrapper-outer').css('margin-bottom', '40px');
				}
				$('.owl-carouselhome').css('display', 'block');
				$('.tab-carousel').css('display','block');
			}

			$('.owl-carouselhome').css('display', 'none');
			if(!isOtherPages){
			var isSpecificPage=$('.owl-carousel__specific').length;
			if(isSpecificPage){
			$('.owl-carousel__specific').owlCarousel({
			    //rtl:true,
			    loop:true,
			    //margin:50,
			    navigation : true,
			    pagination: true,
			    dots:true,
			    singleItem: true,
			    stopOnHover: true,
			    itemsScaleUp : true,
			    autoPlay: 10000, // set false to disable
			    afterInit : showHomepageCarousel,
			    navigationText : ["<span class='icon-arrow-left'></span>","<span class='icon-arrow-right'></span>"],
			    responsive:{
			        0:{
			            items:1
			        },
			        600:{
			            items:1
			        },
			        1000:{
			            items:1
			        }
			    }
			});
			}
			}
			$( window ).resize(function() {
				$(".owl-carousel__specific").each(function(){
					$(this).data('owlCarousel').updateVars();
				});
				$("#proddetaildescription").trigger("update");
			});
			if(isOtherPages){
				showHomepageCarousel();
			}
   }



		});
			</script>

<script>
var isHomePage = $('body').hasClass('page-homepage');
var headerHeight = $('header').height() || 180;
var hasBreadCrumb = $('.breadcrumb-section').length && true;
var windowInnerWidth = window.innerWidth;
var isMobileWindow = windowInnerWidth <= 1023 ? true : false;

if(isHomePage && isMobileWindow) {
	$("#content-container").css('margin-top', headerHeight+24);
}
if(hasBreadCrumb && isMobileWindow) {
	$("#content-container").css('margin-top', headerHeight+7);
}

if(!isHomePage && !hasBreadCrumb && isMobileWindow) {
	$("#content-container").css('margin-top', headerHeight+24);
}

	$("#content-container").css('margin-top', headerHeight+20);
} */
